function OnFocus()
{ 
   
      document.getElementById("ctl00_PlaceHolderSearchArea_uc11_tbQuery").className = "normal";
      //document.getElementById("ctl00_PlaceHolderSearchArea_uc11_tbQuery").value = "";
   
}

function OnBlur()
{
   var textValue = document.getElementById("ctl00_PlaceHolderSearchArea_uc11_tbQuery").value;
    //alert("Hello World!");
   if (textValue.length == 0)
   {
   

      document.getElementById("ctl00_PlaceHolderSearchArea_uc11_tbQuery").className = "watermark";
      
   }
   else
      document.getElementById("ctl00_PlaceHolderSearchArea_uc11_tbQuery").className = "normal";
}

</script>

}

}

       <div id="main"> 
        <h2> Campus Safety Escort Service&nbsp; </h2> 
        <div id="ctl00_PlaceHolderMain_ctl00__ControlWrapper_RichImageField" style="display:inline">
         <span dir=""><img alt="Campus Safety" border="0" src="../../SiteCollectionImages/headerImages/campusSafetyLandingHeader.jpg" style="border:0px solid" /></span>&nbsp;
        </div> 
        <div id="ctl00_PlaceHolderMain_ctl01__ControlWrapper_RichHtmlField" style="display:inline">
         <h4>Using the Campus Escort Service</h4> 
         <p>The Campus Safety Escort Service (CSES) is safe and easy to use. It’s available to students, staff, faculty and anyone else who needs a safety escort. The service is free. There are four ways to get a safety escort: </p> 
         <ul style="width:430px;float:right" class="green"> 
          <li>Pick up any red phone on campus that reads “Campus Safety Escort Service” and it will automatically connect you to the dispatcher desk. You will be connected to the <a title="" href="http://police.ucr.edu/" target="_blank">UCR Police Department </a>when the service is not in operation. </li> 
          <li>Stop by the dispatcher desks at the <a href="http://campusmap.ucr.edu/imap/index.html?loc=HUB">HUB</a> information desk or <a href="http://campusmap.ucr.edu/imap/index.html?loc=RIVL">Rivera Library</a> to request a safety escort in person. </li> 
          <li>Call the dispatcher desk at 951-827-3772. </li> 
          <li>If you see a safety escort on campus (look for the yellow shirt and ID badge), just wave them down and they will walk you to your destination. </li>
         </ul>
         <img style="margin-top:59px" src="../../SiteCollectionImages/redPhone.png" /> 
         <div class="clear"></div> 
         <h4>Location</h4> 
         <p>CSES dispatch desks are located at the <a href="http://campusmap.ucr.edu/imap/index.html?loc=HUB">HUB</a> information desk and inside the <a href="http://campusmap.ucr.edu/imap/index.html?loc=RIVL">Rivera Library</a>. </p> 
         <p>The CSES office is located in the Women’s Resource Center at 260 <a title="" href="http://campusmap.ucr.edu/imap/index.html?loc=COSTH" target="_blank">Costo Hall</a>. The Women’s Resource Center is open 8 a.m.-5 p.m., Monday through Friday. </p> 
         <p>Use our map to <a title="" href="FindtheNearestEscortPhone.aspx">find the nearest Campus Safety Escort Service phone</a>.</p> 
         <h4>Operating Hours </h4> 
         <p>The Campus Safety Escort Service operates from dark to 11:30 p.m., Sunday through Thursday. After 11:30 p.m., call UCR Police at951-827-5222. </p>
        </div> 
       </div>

        <li><a href="http://mesc.ucr.edu">Middle Eastern Student Center</a></li> 
       </ul> 
       <p class="footer_info"> <img width="120" height="103" alt="UCR" src="../../Style%20Library/Images/wrc.jpg" /> <strong>The Women’s Resource Center</strong> is part of UC Riverside's family of ethnic and gender programs. As the 6th most diverse university in the nation (U.S. News and World Report), UC Riverside encourages an atmosphere of respect and celebration of ethnic, gender, and cultural differences. We unite as a community to promote academic and social success for everyone.</p>

    <div id="haunts-header">
        <span>
            From legendary horror classics and modern day fright-fests to campy cult favs, comedic twisters and terrifying slasher sensations, WB.com spotlights more than 80 years of cinematic chills and thrills from the Warner Bros. film library this month. Watch original trailers and discover (or re-discover) 75 spine-tinglers to consider for your personal fright night viewing on All Hallows Eve!
            <a href="/wbhaunts/index.html">Visit our WB Haunts Page</a>
        </span>
    </div>
    <div id="haunts-scroll">
        <div id="haunts-loading"></div>
        <a href="/prev" id="haunts-prev"></a>
        <a href="/next" id="haunts-next"></a>
    </div>
</div>
<script src="//ajax.googleapis.com/ajax/libs/jquery/1.10.2/jquery.min.js"></script>
<script src="//cdnjs.cloudflare.com/ajax/libs/spin.js/1.3.2/spin.min.js"></script>
<script type="text/javascript">
var HauntsTemplate = new Ext.XTemplate('<ul id="haunts-list">',
        '<tpl for="items">',
            '<li>',
                '<a href="{link}" title="{name_orig}">',
                    '<img src="{poster_src}" />',
                    '<span class="name">{name}</span>',
                    '<span class="date">{year}</span>',
                '</a>',
            '</li>',
        '</tpl>',
    '</ul>'
);

var spinner = new Spinner({
    lines: 10,
    length: 8,
    width: 4,
    radius: 8,
    corners: 1,
    color: "#fff"
}).spin($("#haunts-loading").show().get(0));

Ext.Ajax.request({
    url: "/api/CONTENT/WarnerBros.com/wbhaunts/titles.json?field_filter=name,usTheatricalDate,posters,parentId&sort_field=caption,ASC",
    success: function (response, opts) {
        var result = Ext.util.JSON.decode(response.responseText);
        if (result.items) {
            var i, l = result.items.length,
                movie, posters;
                
            for (i = 0; i < l; i++) {
                movie = result.items[i];
                
                // Get movie link
                movie.link = "/wbhaunts/" + titleToSlug(movie.name) + "/" + movie.parentId + ".html";
                
                // Get movie poster
                posters = movie.posters[0];
                if (posters.posterScroll) {
                    movie.poster_src = posters.posterScroll.upload || posters.posterScroll.url;
                } else if (posters.posterLarge) {
                    movie.poster_src = posters.posterLarge.upload || posters.posterLarge.url;
                }
                
                // Get movie name
                movie.name_orig = movie.name;
                movie.name = titleFix(movie.name.toLowerCase());
                
                // Get movie year
                movie.year = movie.usTheatricalDate.substr(0, 4);
                
                result.items[i] = movie;
            }
            
            $(function () {
                HauntsTemplate.append(Ext.getDom("haunts-scroll"), result);
                spinner.stop();
                $("#haunts-loading").hide();
                $("a#haunts-next").show();
            });
        }
    }
});

$(function () {
    var offset = 885,
        animating = false;
    
    $("a#haunts-prev").click(function (e) {
        e.preventDefault();
        
        if (!animating) {
            animating = true;
        
            var destination = $("#haunts-list").position().left + offset;
            $("#haunts-list").animate({
                left: destination
            }, 300, function () {
                animating = false;
            });
            
            if (destination + offset > 50) {
                $(this).hide();
            }
            
            $("a#haunts-next").show();
        }
    });
    
    $("a#haunts-next").click(function (e) {
        e.preventDefault();
        
        if (!animating) {
            animating = true;
        
            var destination = $("#haunts-list").position().left - offset,
                width = $("#haunts-list").width();
            
            $("#haunts-list").animate({
                left: destination
            }, 300, function () {
                animating = false;
            });
            
            if (width - Math.abs(destination - offset) < offset) {
                $(this).hide();
            }
            
            $("a#haunts-prev").show();
        }
    });
});
</script>-->

    ytpreload.getSnapClass = function(guidePinned) {
      var SCROLLBAR_WIDTH = 21;
      var CONTENT_PADDING = 50;
      var GUIDE_WIDTH = 230;
      var SNAP_WIDTH_2 = 1056;
      var SNAP_WIDTH_3 = 1262;

          document.documentElement.clientWidth;

        return ytpreload.SnapClassList[1];
      } else {

      }

        // Google WaterMark Script
        $(function () {
            $("#txtGoogleSearch").each(function () {
                ToggleHint($(this)); // add class on page load to elements with "hintable" class
            });

            $("#txtGoogleSearch").focus(function () {
                $(this).removeClass("GoogleWatermark"); // handle all focus hints
            });

            $("#txtGoogleSearch").blur(function () {
                ToggleHint(this); // handle all blur hints
            });
        });

        function ToggleHint(obj) {
            if ($(obj).val() == '') { $(obj).addClass("GoogleWatermark"); };
        }
    </script>

     <img src="/Images/one-time-events.png" alt="" class="page-lead" /> 
     <div class="span-11"> 
      <h3>Reserve a Room for a One-Time Event</h3> 
      <p>Faculty and Staff may reserve a classroom for an academic-related event such as a review session, film screening or guest speaker.</p> 
      <p>If you need a room for a conference or symposium, or a nonacademic event (e.g., student organization meeting, retirement party, etc.), please contact <a href="http://hub.ucr.edu/EventScheduling/Pages/CommonsEventScheduling.aspx">Highlander Event Scheduling.</a></p> 
      <p>Events with food also go through <a href="http://hub.ucr.edu/EventScheduling/Pages/CommonsEventScheduling.aspx">Highlander Event Scheduling</a> as we cannot provide custodial service.</p> 
      <h4>Explore Available Rooms</h4> 
     </div> 
     <div class="span-7 last"> 
      <div class="sidebar"> 
       <img src="/Images/paperpushpin.png" style="float: right; margin: 4px;" /> 
       <div class="title">
         Helpful Resources: 
       </div> 
       <ul class="helpfulResourcesImage"> 
        <li><a href="http://classrooms.ucr.edu/index.php">Smart Classrooms</a></li> 
        <li><a href="http://hub.ucr.edu/EventScheduling/Pages/CommonsEventScheduling.aspx">Highlander Event Scheduling</a></li> 
        <li><a href="http://cnc.ucr.edu/multimedia/">Multimedia Technologies</a></li> 
        <li><a href="http://rspace.ucr.edu">R'Space</a></li> 
        <li><a href="/crams/default.aspx">CRAMS</a></li> 
       </ul> 
      </div> 
     </div> 
     <div class="span-17 last"> 
      <p>Explore classrooms, seating capacities and media options with <a href="http://classrooms.ucr.edu/index.php">Smart Classrooms</a>.</p> 
      <h4>Reserve a Room</h4> 
      <p>Email <a href="mailto:margaret.stewart@ucr.edu">Margaret Stewart</a> with a request that includes:</p> 
      <ul class="orange-bullets wide" style="font-weight: bold;"> 
       <li>Your event name</li> 
       <li>The connected academic course</li> 
       <li>Event date(s)</li> 
       <li>Start and end time(s)</li> 
       <li>Number of rooms needed</li> 
       <li>Room size needed</li> 
       <li>If you have a specific classroom in mind, please tell us which one</li> 
      </ul> 
      <p>Room requests for events after 6 p.m. and on weekends can be processed up to six months in advance. Events before 6 p.m. (M-F) can be scheduled after the second week of the quarter.</p> 
      <p>Visit <a href="http://classrooms.ucr.edu/index.php">Smart Classrooms</a> to see media technology available in each general assignment classroom.</p> 
      <p>To request a classroom with specific technology for ongoing academic activities (lectures, etc.), please see <a href="scheduling-academic-course-activities.aspx">Scheduling Academic Course Activities</a>.</p> 
      <h4>Reservation Confirmation</h4> 
      <p>If your request can be accommodated, you will receive an email confirming your reservation. If it cannot, you will receive an email to that effect (usually with suggestions for alternative rooms).</p> 
      <p>The start time of your event will reflect a 10-minute passing time (e.g., 9:10 a.m. if 9 a.m. is requested).</p> 
      <h4>Early Media Set Up</h4> 
      <p>If you need to get into the classroom early to set up any equipment, please contact Multimedia Technologies at (951) 827-3041 or <a href="mailto:multimedia@ucr.edu">multimedia@ucr.edu</a>.</p> 
      <h4>Locked Out?</h4> 
      <p>When you reserve a room, we take steps to make sure it will be unlocked for you. However, sometimes doors get locked accidentally. Call our office (during office hours) and we can help you. If your event takes place after 4:30 p.m. or on the weekend, contact UCR Police at (951) 827-5222 and they can unlock the door for you. Be sure to have your email confirmation or room permit to show the officer on duty!</p> 
      <p>&nbsp;</p> 
     </div> 
    </div> 
   </div>

    <h2>Computing Infrastructure &amp; Security</h2> 
    <!-- Start Sidebar --> 
    <div id="sidebar"> 
     <div class="nav"> 
      <h3 class="accessibility">Main Navigation</h3> 
      <ul> 
       <li><a href="/" title="Home">Home<br /><span></span></a></li>

    <!-- Start Content Area --> 
    <div id="main"> 
     <!-- com.omniupdate.editor csspath="/z-omniupdate/css/macy.css" cssmenu="" width="790" --> 
     <div class="header"> 
      <!-- com.omniupdate.div label="title" group="Everyone" button="734" -->
      <!-- com.omniupdate.editor csspath="/z-omniupdate/css/style.css" cssmenu="/z-omniupdate/css/style.txt" width="484" --> 
      <!-- /com.omniupdate.div -->
     </div> 
     <div id="omnicontent"> 
      <!-- com.omniupdate.div label="maincontent" group="Everyone" button="657" -->
      <!-- com.omniupdate.editor csspath="/z-omniupdate/css/style.css" cssmenu="/z-omniupdate/css/style.txt" width="484" --> 
      <p>Computing Infrastructure &amp; Security (CIS) provides computing systems infrastructure, identity management, and security support to Computing and Communications (C&amp;C) and the campus.</p> 
      <p>Infrastructure support includes system setup and maintenance, including backups, and system administration. The infrastructure supported systems provide enterprise services to the campus, including mail and calendaring, ilearn, and web hosting, as well as basic services such as DNS, LDAP and Active Directory.</p> 
      <p>Identity management support includes running the technologies that provide single sign on, federated service access, and multi-factor authentication.</p> 
      <p>Security support includes monitoring campus network health, reducing the number of external intruders, and providing guidance for campus server security standards.</p> 
      <h3>Mission Statement</h3> 
      <p>Provide the best possible infrastructure, identity, and security services to meet business needs given budget realities.</p> 
      <h3>Projects</h3> 
      <h4>Security</h4> 
      <ul> 
       <li>Safe Campus Network Environment</li> 
       <li>Provide Auditable Security for Critical Campus Systems</li> 
       <li>Detect Campus Threats Before They Cause Damage</li> 
       <li>Prevent Security Incidents From Spreading</li> 
       <li>Payment Card Industry Compliant Credit Card Processing</li> 
      </ul> 
      <h4>Identity Management and Middleware Services</h4> 
      <ul> 
       <li>Allow All Campus Users to Access UCR and other Applications with One Login</li> 
       <li>Provision Accounts Immediately Upon Faculty/Staff/Student Arrival</li> 
       <li>Remove Account After Faculty/Staff/Student Depart</li> 
       <li>Maintain, Create, Change Individual Attributes (e.g. student status, major, etc.) in Campus Directory Server</li> 
       <li>Support best practice, secure, password management</li> 
      </ul> 
      <h4>Research Computing and Cyber-Infrastructure</h4> 
      <ul> 
       <li>C&amp;C server system administration</li> 
       <li>Server configuration management</li> 
       <li>Robust backup service for C&amp;C servres</li> 
       <li>Monitor C&amp;C servers for service disruptions</li> 
       <li>Support and maintain DHCP, DNS, LDAP, Active Directory, TACACS, NTP</li> 
      </ul> 
      <h4>Shared Services</h4> 
      <ul> 
       <li>Web Hosting for Academic Departments, Colleges, Faculty</li> 
       <li>Faculty Time Share (shared access to systems for general purpose needs)</li> 
      </ul> 
      <h4>Collaboration Services</h4> 
      <ul> 
       <li>E-Mail and Campus Calendar System</li> 
       <li>Campus Learning Management System</li> 
       <li>Faculty, Staff Files Sharing and Instant Messaging</li> 
      </ul> 
      <h4>Disaster Recovery</h4> 
      <ul> 
       <li>Manage Systems To Save Data In A Safe, Recoverable Manner</li> 
       <li>Manage Hardware Inventory For Recovery From Disaster</li> 
      </ul>
